(Virtual smartcards are cards stored on a smartphone or tablet.)\r\n\r\nGo Smart is an app that allows you to check a cardholder’s details using an NFC card reader or via a device’s camera by reading a QR code. \r\n\r\nYour device reads information either directly from the smartcard’s chip electronically or from a virtual smartcard’s secure, short-life QR Code and then surfaces this on your screen. This not only reduces the possibility of card fraud, but also makes capturing and storing smartcard details much quicker and more efficient. \r\n\r\nThis app works online, accessing the most up-to-date information, as well as offline. So, if you cannot get a phone signal, you can still read the data on the physical smartcard or access the basic details from the virtual smartcard’s QR Code that proves the smartcard is genuine. \r\n\r\n\r\nUsage details for the Windows Mobile version:\r\n\r\nPlease note that this app requires newer models of the Lumia range, which use the enhanced NFC chipset (PN547) e.g. Lumia 735 or 830. (If the photo shown does not match the one shown on the front of the actual card, it has probably been tampered with and may be a fake card.);\r\n5.\tTouch the Card Details tab to view the list of current qualifications.\r\n6.\tDo the same with more smartcards if you need to.\r\n\r\n\r\nTo read a virtual smartcard:\r\n\r\n1.\tOpen the app;\r\n2.\tTouch the 'SCAN A QR CODE' button;\r\n3.\tRead the QR code (from approx. 10cm away);\r\n4.\tAn image of the card appears. (If the photo shown does not match the one on the cardholder’s phone, it is a fake card.);\r\n5.\tTouch the card image to view the back of the card;\r\n6.\tTouch the Core Data tab to view qualifications;\r\n7.\tTouch the SkillSight tab, if one is present, to view further qualifications for the cardholder;\r\n8.\tRepeat this process to read more virtual smartcards.
